			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">NEWPORT BEACH, Calf. &#x2013; February 4, 2020 &#x2013; Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) today reported financial results for its fourth quarter and fiscal year ended December 31, 2019.</font>

			<a name="_Hlk30676915"></a><a name="_Hlk504391754"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&#x201C;We had a strong ending to 2019 as Q4 marks the eighth-consecutive quarter of accelerating comparable sales, which highlights that running great restaurants with the right leaders and the right culture is delivering outstanding financial performance,&#x201D; said Brian Niccol, Chief Executive Officer, Chipotle.&nbsp;&#x201C;</font><a name="_Hlk536635139"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">For the full year, Chipotle&#x2019;s average unit volumes </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">exceeded $2.2 million and digital sales surpassed a billion dollars, showing that our key strategies are working, and the Chipotle brand is thriving as we build a sustainable model that helps cultivate a better world.&#x201D;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

</div><hr size="3" style="color:#999999" width="100%" align="center"></hr><p style="page-break-after:always">&nbsp;</p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font>

		</p>

</div>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;">Fourth quarter 2019 results:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Revenue for the quarter was $1.4 billion, an increase of 17.6% from the fourth quarter of 2018. The increase in revenue was driven by a 13.4% increase in comparable restaurant sales and new restaurant openings. Comparable restaurant sales included no net impact from our rewards program as deferred revenue was essentially offset by redemptions and a refined breakage rate assumption for chips and guacamole. Comparable restaurant sales improved primarily as a result of an 8.0% transaction growth, as well as a 5.4% increase in the average check.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">We opened a record 80 new restaurants including </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">one</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> relocation during the quarter and closed </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">three</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. This included 46 Chipotlanes resulting in a total of 66 Chipotlanes at year-end. For 2020, we anticipate opening 150-165 new restaurants with more than half including a Chipotlane.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Food, beverage and packaging costs were 33.1% of revenue, a decrease of 10 bps compared to the fourth quarter of 2018. The decrease was primarily due to the benefit of menu price increases and to a lesser extent favorable avocado pricing, partially offset by increased costs of several other ingredients, including carne asada and expenses related to loyalty.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Restaurant level operating margin was 19.2% in the quarter, an improvement from 17.0% in the fourth quarter of 2018.&nbsp; The improvement was driven primarily by leverage from the comparable restaurant sales increase, partially offset by wage inflation at the crew level and increased delivery expense. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">General and administrative expenses were&nbsp;$112.4 million&nbsp;on a GAAP basis, or&nbsp;$106.4 million&nbsp;on a non-GAAP basis, excluding&nbsp;$3.6 million net related to several legal matters and&nbsp;$2.3 million&nbsp;related to transformation expenses. Included in the legal matters this quarter was a $10 million reserve related to the US Attorney&#x2019;s investigation that began in January 2016. This brings the total reserve to $25 million</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;We believe this amount is a reasonable estimate of what we may be expected to pay to settle this </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">matter. While there can be no assurance that a settlement will be reached, we have been cooperating with the investigation and are in discussions to resolve this matter. GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the fourth quarter of 2019 also included underlying general and administrative expenses totaling&nbsp;$74.9 million,&nbsp;$25.4 million&nbsp;related to non-cash stock compensation,&nbsp;$4.5 million&nbsp;related to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher bonus accruals from our strong operating performance and payroll taxes, and&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;related to our upcoming All Manager Conference.&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> GAAP</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> effective tax rate was 28.3% in the fourth quarter of 2019, compared to 26.3% in the fourth quarter of 2018.&nbsp;The increase was primarily due to current year increases in non-deductible executive compensation.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> On a non-GAAP basis, the 2019 fourth quarter effective tax rate was 27.0%.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income for the fourth quarter of 2019</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$72.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$2.55</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, compared to net income of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$32.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$1.15</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, in the fourth quarter of 2018. Excluding the impact of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">legal expenses, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">corporate restructuring, and certain other costs, adjusted net income was $81.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and adjusted diluted earnings per share was $2.86.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">During the quarter, o</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ur Board of Directors approved the investment of up to an additional $100 million, exclusive of commissions, to repurchase shares of our common stock, subject to market conditions.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">This repurchase authorization, in addition to approximately $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">69.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million available as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">December</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> 31, 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> for repurchases under a previously announced repurchase authorization, may be modified, suspended, or discontinued at any time.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Full year 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;"> results</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">:</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Revenue for 2019 was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$5.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> billion, an increase of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">14.8%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> from 2018. The increase in revenue was driven by a 11.1% increase in comparable restaurant sales net of 20 bps from loyalty deferral, and new restaurant openings. Comparable restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">improved primarily as a result of a 7.0% transaction growth, as well as a 4.1% increase in the average check. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">We opened </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">40 new restaurants during the year, including </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">two</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> relocation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, and closed </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">seven</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, in-line with previous guidance, bringing the total restaurant count at year-end to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2,622</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Food, beverage and packaging costs were </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">33.1%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> of revenue, a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">n increase</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;b</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ps</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> compared to 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">crease was driven by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher costs of several ingredients including carne asada, dairy, avocados, and expenses related to loyalty, partially offset by the benefit of menu price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20.5%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> for 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, an improvement from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">18.7%</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> in 201</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The improvement was driven primarily by leverage from the comparable restaurant sales increase, partially offset by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">higher food costs, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">wage inflation at the crew </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">level</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, increased delivery expense, and increased marketing spend</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">General and administrative expenses were&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">451.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;on a GAAP basis, or&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">406.9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;on a non-GAAP basis, excluding&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">30.8</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> net</font><font style="display: inline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">related to several </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">legal matters and&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">13.9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;related to transformation expenses</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, restaurant closure costs and certain other costs</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. GAAP and non-GAAP general and administrative expenses for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">full year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> also include</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">d</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> underlying general and administrative expenses totaling&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">293.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million,&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">90.4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;related to non-cash stock compensation,&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">19.3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;related to higher bonus accruals from our strong operating performance and payroll taxes, and&nbsp;$</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">4.2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million&nbsp;related to our upcoming All Manager Conference.&nbsp;</font><a name="_Hlk505335379"></a>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">GAAP </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">effective tax rate was 23.6% in 2019, compared to 34.2% in 2018.&nbsp;The decrease was primarily due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">excess benefits from stock-based compensation and a year over year decrease in tax expense related to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">expirations of stock-based awards</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, partially offset by current year increases in non-deductible executive compensation.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> On a non-GAAP basis, the 2019 full year effective tax rate was 22.4%.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Net income for 2019 was </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$350.2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$12.38</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share, compared to net income of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$176.6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million, or </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">$6.31</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> per diluted share for 2018. Excluding the impact of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">legal expenses, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">corporate restructuring, restaurant asset impairment, and certain other costs, adjusted net income was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">397.7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> million and adjusted diluted earnings per share was $</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">14</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Average restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">refers to the average trailing 12-month sales for restaurants in operation for at least 12 full calendar months.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>

		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">conference</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> call can be accessed live over the phone by dialing 1-888-317-6003 or for international callers by dialing 1-412-317-6061 and use code: 7638969. The call will be webcast live from the company's website on the investor relations page at ir.chipotle.com/events. An archived webcast will be available approximately one hour after the end of the call.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had over 2,600 restaurants as of December 30, 2019, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. With more than 83,000 employees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the food industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. Steve Ells, founder and executive chairman, first opened Chipotle with a single restaurant in Denver, Colorado in 1993. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">Certain statements in this press release, including statements under the heading &#x201C;Outlook&#x201D; about our anticipated comparable restaurant sales, effective tax rate and estimated number of new restaurant openings in 2020, are forward-looking statements as defined in the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. We use words such as &#x201C;anticipate&#x201D;, &#x201C;believe&#x201D;, &#x201C;could&#x201D;, &#x201C;should&#x201D;, &#x201C;estimate&#x201D;, &#x201C;expect&#x201D;, &#x201C;intend&#x201D;, &#x201C;project&#x201D;, &#x201C;target&#x201D;, and similar terms and phrases, including references to assumptions, to identify forward-looking statements. The forward-looking statements in this press release are based on currently available operating, financial and competitive information available to us as of the date of this release and we assume no obligation to update these forward-looking statements. These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: risks of food safety and food-borne illnesses and other health concerns about our food; risks associated with our reliance on certain information technology systems and potential failures or interruptions; privacy and cyber security risks related to our acceptance of electronic payments or electronic processing of confidential customer or employee information; the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the increasingly competitive labor market and our ability to attract and retain qualified employees; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, restaurant design and construction, or the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due to our Food With Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers&#x2019; perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased overall consumer spending, or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our increased focus on our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions related to food safety incidents and potential class action litigation regarding employment laws, advertising claims or other matters; and other risk factors described from time to time in our SEC reports, including our annual report on Form 10-K and quarterly reports on Form 10-Q, all of which are available on the investor relations page of our website at ir.Chipotle.com.</font>

Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding distinct legal proceedings and transformation expenses. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, and adjusted general and administrative expenses measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
